* **IMMZD2DTDTPOnTimeStartLogic**

## Library: IMMZD2DTDTPOnTimeStartLogic 

| | |
| :--- | :--- |
| *Official URL*:http://smart.who.int/immunizations/Library/IMMZD2DTDTPOnTimeStartLogic | *Version*:1.0.0 |
| Draft as of 2026-04-09 | *Computable Name*:IMMZD2DTDTPOnTimeStartLogic |

 
This library defines decision support logic for the IMMZ.D2.DT.DTP.On-time start decision table in the Immunization CPG 

* * **Content: **text/cql: ````/* * Library: IMMZD2DTDTPOnTimeStartLogic (IMMZ.D2.DT.DTP.On-time start) * Rule: Determine if the client is due for a diphtheria–tetanus–pertussis (DTP) vaccination according to the national immunization schedule * Decision Table: DTP vaccination schedule, on-time start (at ≤ 12 months of age) * Trigger: IMMZ.D2 Determine required vaccination(s) if any */ library IMMZD2DTDTPOnTimeStartLogic using FHIR version '4.0.1' include FHIRHelpers version '4.0.1' include IMMZD2DTDTPEncounterElements called Encounter parameter Today Date default Today() context Patient /* @dynamicValue: Guidance */ define "Guidance": case // Handling overlaps for Pertussis and Td boosters. when "Primary DTP series is complete.
